     832             : 
     833             : /*
     834             :  * Identity remapping. Not for casual consumers.
     835             :  *
     836             :  * Normally, an object's contents and its identity are inextricably linked.
     837             :  * Identity is determined by the address of the JSObject* in the heap, and
     838             :  * the contents are what is located at that address. Transplanting allows these
     839             :  * concepts to be separated through a combination of swapping (exchanging the
     840             :  * contents of two same-compartment objects) and remapping cross-compartment
     841             :  * identities by altering wrappers.
     842             :  *
     843             :  * The |origobj| argument should be the object whose identity needs to be
     844             :  * remapped, usually to another compartment. The contents of |origobj| are
     845             :  * destroyed.
     846             :  *
     847             :  * The |target| argument serves two purposes:
     848             :  *
     849             :  * First, |target| serves as a hint for the new identity of the object. The new
     850             :  * identity object will always be in the same compartment as |target|, but
     851             :  * if that compartment already had an object representing |origobj| (either a
     852             :  * cross-compartment wrapper for it, or |origobj| itself if the two arguments
     853             :  * are same-compartment), the existing object is used. Otherwise, |target|
     854             :  * itself is used. To avoid ambiguity, JS_TransplantObject always returns the
     855             :  * new identity.
     856             :  *
     857             :  * Second, the new identity object's contents will be those of |target|. A swap()
     858             :  * is used to make this happen if an object other than |target| is used.
     859             :  *
     860             :  * We don't have a good way to recover from failure in this function, so
     861             :  * we intentionally crash instead.
     862             :  */
     863             :

    6820             : // Fast path to get the activation to use for GetScriptedCallerGlobal. If this
    6821             : // returns false, the fast path didn't work out and the caller has to use the

    6826             : // so if an activation contains at least one non-self-hosted frame, we can use
